FuriousRamsayNPCControl_title,Quest,Quest Info,"Controlling your NPC Hires"
FuriousRamsayNPCControl,Quest,Quest Info,"In the event you're not too antisocial, there are some survivors that will work for you... for a price.\n\nI've given you a couple commands you can use from your toolbelt. Both are toggles. Press them to cycle through the various options. By default your hires will hunt down everything (Hunting Mode). You have no control over them, they're stubborn.\n\nIn Threat Control Mode they will refrain from attacking any type of hostile animal. In Full control mode they won't attack at all. In both of these last two modes they will engage hostiles if you get hurt or if you start attacking.\n\nThe second command (Stop) will only work in the last two modes. They will halt all current attacks or will resume attacking when you toggle this command. This can be useful if you need to run and force them to follow you. Just don't forget to that they won't help unless you eventually tell them to Resume.\n\n - Briston"

quest_FuriousRamsaySurpriseTier1_offer,Quests,Quests,"This is a solo mission as this has to be kept quiet. Go to [DECEA3]{poi.name}[-] and leave the Duke and his Trader Network a surprise they won't soon forget.\n\nWe desperately need some of their weapons, so you'll only be able to open the backpack you'll start with after you've retrieved those hidden supplies. That's the priority.\n\nFollowing the retrieval, you'll have 45 seconds to open the backpack and lay down an explosive charge... then another 30 seconds to lay down three mines as added insurance.\n\nOnce a charge is set, it'll blow about 10 seconds after, so make sure to be at least 10 meters away from the blast zone.\n\nCan't lay down the mines without setting the charge first, and we'll know. We always know."
